   <!-- Wikia Beacon Tracking -->
   <script>
    require(['wikia.trackingOptIn'], function (trackingOptIn) {
 		trackingOptIn.pushToUserConsentQueue(function (optIn) {
 			function genUID() {
 				return 'xxxxxxxx-xxxx-4xxx-yxxx-xxxxxxxxxxxx'.replace(/[xy]/g, function (c) {
 					var r = Math.random() * 16 | 0, v = c === 'x' ? r : (r & 0x3 | 0x8);
 					return v.toString(16);
 				});
 			}
 
 			function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
 				var cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
 
 				return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
 			}
 
 			var expireDate = new Date(),
 					beacon = getCookieValue('wikia_beacon_id'),
 					script = document.createElement('script'),
 					utma = getCookieValue('__utma'),
 					utmb = getCookieValue('__utmb'),
 					trackUrl,
 					sessionId = getCookieValue('tracking_session_id'),
 					pvNumber = getCookieValue('pv_number'),
 					pvNumberGlobal = getCookieValue('pv_number_global');
 
 			if (beacon) {
 				window.beacon_id = beacon;
 			} else {
 				// something went terribly wrong
 				try {
 					var request = new XMLHttpRequest(),
 							data = {
 								name: 'MediaWiki.track',
 								description: 'wikia_beacon_id is empty',
 								client: 'oasis'
 							};
 					request.open('POST', 'https://services.wikia.com/event-logger/error', true);
 					request.setRequestHeader('Content-type', 'application/json');
 					request.send(JSON.stringify(data));
 				} catch (error) {
 					// Ignore error sending log request
 				}
 			}
 
 			window.sessionId = sessionId ? sessionId : genUID();
 			window.pvNumber = pvNumber ? parseInt(pvNumber, 10) + 1 : 1;
 			window.pvNumberGlobal = pvNumberGlobal ? parseInt(pvNumberGlobal, 10) + 1 : 1;
 			window.pvUID = genUID();
 
 			expireDate = new Date(expireDate.getTime() + 1000 * 60 * 30);
 			document.cookie = 'tracking_session_id=' + window.sessionId + '; expires=' + expireDate.toGMTString() +
 					';domain=' + window.wgCookieDomain + '; path=' + window.wgCookiePath + ';';
 			document.cookie = 'pv_number=' + window.pvNumber + '; expires=' + expireDate.toGMTString() +
 					'; path=' + window.wgCookiePath + ';';
 			document.cookie = 'pv_number_global=' + window.pvNumberGlobal + '; expires=' + expireDate.toGMTString() +
 					';domain=' + window.wgCookieDomain + '; path=' + window.wgCookiePath + ';';

         <div class="mw-content-ltr mw-content-text" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en">
          <div class="main-page-tag-lcs main-page-tag-lcs-exploded">
           <div class="lcs-container">
            <div class="plainlinks" style="text-align: center;">
             <p>
              <big>
               <b>
                Welcome to WikIkariam
               </b>
              </big>
             </p>
             <p>
              The wiki about
              <a href="/wiki/Gameforge" title="Gameforge">
               Gameforge
              </a>
              's browser game
              <a href="/wiki/Ikariam" title="Ikariam">
               Ikariam
              </a>
              that
              <a href="/wiki/Help:Editing" title="Help:Editing">
               anyone can edit
              </a>
              .
             </p>
             <div class="center">
              <div class="floatnone">
               <a class="image image-thumbnail link-internal" href="/wiki/Ikariam" title="WikIkariam, the Ikariam wiki">
                <img alt="WikIkariam Main Logo" class="lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="WikIkariam_Main_Logo.png" data-image-name="WikIkariam Main Logo.png" data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/d/d5/WikIkariam_Main_Logo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/670?cb=20090613185300" height="130" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="670"/>
                <noscript>
                 <img alt="WikIkariam Main Logo" class="" data-image-key="WikIkariam_Main_Logo.png" data-image-name="WikIkariam Main Logo.png" height="130" src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/d/d5/WikIkariam_Main_Logo.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/670?cb=20090613185300" width="670"/>
                </noscript>
               </a>
              </div>
             </div>
             <p>
              Since February 17
              <sup>
               th
              </sup>
              , 2008 we have added over
              <a href="/wiki/Special:AllPages" title="Special:AllPages">
               1,313 articles
              </a>
              to this wiki.
             </p>
             <p>
              We currently have
              <a href="/wiki/Special:ActiveUsers" title="Special:ActiveUsers">
               5 active users
              </a>
              working on the site.
              <br/>
              We have a total of 2
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Sysop" title="Sysop">
               Administrators
              </a>
              , of whom 6 are
              <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bureaucrat" title="Bureaucrat">
               Bureaucrats
              </a>
              .
              <br/>
              <small>
               Click
               <a href="/wiki/Special:Statistics" title="Special:Statistics">
                here
               </a>
               for more statistics.
              </small>
             </p>
             <p>
              This wiki is best viewed with a
              <b>
               modern browser
              </b>
              using the screen size of
              <b>
               1280 x 1024
              </b>
              or larger.
              <br/>
              <small>
               <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WikIkariam" title="WikIkariam">
                We
               </a>
               recommend using the
               <a class="extiw" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Firefox" title="wikipedia:Firefox">
                <b>
                 Firefox browser
                </b>
               </a>
               , because it has a wider
               <i>
                <u>
                 mouse-over
                </u>
                <u>
                 tool-tip
                </u>
               </i>
               space
              </small>
              .
             </p>
            </div>

                     <img alt="Cn-Tw" class="thumbborder lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Cn-Tw.png" data-image-name="Cn-Tw.png" data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/5/51/Cn-Tw.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20120130165041" height="13" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="20"/>
                     <noscript>
                      <img alt="Cn-Tw" class="thumbborder " data-image-key="Cn-Tw.png" data-image-name="Cn-Tw.png" height="13" src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/5/51/Cn-Tw.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20120130165041" width="20"/>
                     </noscript>
                    </a>
                    )
                   </span>

             <div class="plainlinks">
              <h2 style="padding: 0.2em 0.4em; margin: 0 0 10px 0; border: 1px solid #EEC; background: #FEA; color: #DC8; font-weight: bold; font-size: 120%;">
               <span class="mw-headline" id="Ikariam_Game_News">
                Ikariam Game News
               </span>
              </h2>
              <table class="plainlinks" style="width: 100%; margin: auto;">
               <caption>
               </caption>
               <tr>
                <td style="vertical-align: top;">
                 <h2>
                  <span class="mw-headline" id="May_23.2C_2018">
                   May 23, 2018
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <p>
                  <b>
                   New
                   <u>
                    War
                   </u>
                   Servers
                  </b>
                  :
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  <i>
                   All communities'
                  </i>
                  with the exceptions of
                  <span style="white-space: nowrap;">
                   <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/7/70/Fi.png/revision/latest?cb=20120130162539" title="Finland / Republic of Finland / Suomen tasavalta / Republiken Finland">
                    <img alt="Fi" class="thumbborder lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Fi.png" data-image-name="Fi.png" data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/7/70/Fi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20120130162539" height="12" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="20"/>
                    <noscript>
                     <img alt="Fi" class="thumbborder " data-image-key="Fi.png" data-image-name="Fi.png" height="12" src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/7/70/Fi.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20120130162539" width="20"/>
                    </noscript>
                   </a>
                   <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Finland" title="Republic of Finland">
                    FI
                   </a>
                  </span>
                  ,
                  <span style="white-space: nowrap;">
                   <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/9/98/Nl.png/revision/latest?cb=20120130174144" title="Kingdom of the Netherlands / Koninkrijk der Nederlanden / Keninkryk fan de Nederlannen / Reino Hulandes">
                    <img alt="Nl" class="thumbborder lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Nl.png" data-image-name="Nl.png" data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/9/98/Nl.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20120130174144" height="13" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="20"/>
                    <noscript>
                     <img alt="Nl" class="thumbborder " data-image-key="Nl.png" data-image-name="Nl.png" height="13" src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/9/98/Nl.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20120130174144" width="20"/>
                    </noscript>
                   </a>
                   <a href="/wiki/Netherlands" title="Netherlands">
                    NL
                   </a>
                  </span>
                  and
                  <span style="white-space: nowrap;">
                   <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/0/04/No.png/revision/latest?cb=20080701162437" title="Norway / Kingdom of Norway / Kongeriket Norge / Kongeriket Noreg">
                    <img alt="No" class="thumbborder lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="No.png" data-image-name="No.png" data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/0/04/No.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20080701162437" height="15" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="20"/>
                    <noscript>
                     <img alt="No" class="thumbborder " data-image-key="No.png" data-image-name="No.png" height="15" src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/0/04/No.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/20?cb=20080701162437" width="20"/>
                    </noscript>
                   </a>
                   <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Norway" title="Kingdom of Norway">
                    NO
                   </a>
                  </span>
                  have gained
                  <span style="white-space: nowrap;">
                   <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/c/c4/Ares.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120716032449" title="s203 / m203 / War server #2">
                    <img alt="Ares" class="thumbborder lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Ares.jpg" data-image-name="Ares.jpg" data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/c/c4/Ares.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/10?cb=20120716032449" height="20" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="10"/>
                    <noscript>
                     <img alt="Ares" class="thumbborder " data-image-key="Ares.jpg" data-image-name="Ares.jpg" height="20" src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/c/c4/Ares.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/10?cb=20120716032449" width="10"/>
                    </noscript>
                   </a>
                   <a href="/wiki/Category:War_2_servers" title="Category:War 2 servers">
                    War 2
                   </a>
                   (s203)
                  </span>
                 </p>
                 <dl>
                  <dt>
                   Notes:
                  </dt>
                 </dl>
                 <ol>
                  <li>
                   This server will have the following
                   <b>
                    <u>
                     SHARED
                    </u>
                   </b>
                   features, when compared to
                   <span style="white-space: nowrap;">
                    <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/c/c4/Ares.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120716032449" title="s201 / m201 / War server #1">
                     <img alt="Ares" class="thumbborder lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Ares.jpg" data-image-name="Ares.jpg" data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/c/c4/Ares.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/10?cb=20120716032449" height="20" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="10"/>
                     <noscript>
                      <img alt="Ares" class="thumbborder " data-image-key="Ares.jpg" data-image-name="Ares.jpg" height="20" src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/c/c4/Ares.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/10?cb=20120716032449" width="10"/>
                     </noscript>
                    </a>
                    <a href="/wiki/Category:War_1_servers" title="Category:War 1 servers">
                     War 1
                    </a>
                    (s201)
                   </span>
                   :
                   <ol>
                    <li>
                     The building speed of units and buildings is three times as fast.
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     The movement speed of all military units and merchant ships is three times as fast.
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     The production of research points is three times as high.
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     The start level of all resources is level five.
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     The resource production of the saw mill and the luxury mines is three times as high.
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     The effects of the morale feature is deactivated.
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     Gold can be pillaged from other players.
                    </li>
                   </ol>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   This server will have the following
                   <b>
                    <u>
                     UNIQUE
                    </u>
                   </b>
                   features, when compared to
                   <span style="white-space: nowrap;">
                    <a class="image image-thumbnail" href="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/c/c4/Ares.jpg/revision/latest?cb=20120716032449" title="s201 / m201 / War server #1">
                     <img alt="Ares" class="thumbborder lzy lzyPlcHld " data-image-key="Ares.jpg" data-image-name="Ares.jpg" data-src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/c/c4/Ares.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/10?cb=20120716032449" height="20" onload="if(typeof ImgLzy==='object'){ImgLzy.load(this)}" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" width="10"/>
                     <noscript>
                      <img alt="Ares" class="thumbborder " data-image-key="Ares.jpg" data-image-name="Ares.jpg" height="20" src="https://vignette.wikia.nocookie.net/ikariam/images/c/c4/Ares.jpg/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/10?cb=20120716032449" width="10"/>
                     </noscript>
                    </a>
                    <a href="/wiki/Category:War_1_servers" title="Category:War 1 servers">
                     War 1
                    </a>
                    (s201)
                   </span>
                   :
                   <ol>
                    <li>
                     This server has reduced:
                     <ol>
                      <li>
                       Training and travel times for spies.
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Cooldowns and durations of miracles.
                      </li>
                     </ol>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     This server has increased:
                     <ol>
                      <li>
                       Fallback times.
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Loading times - including with pillaging.
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Building times.
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Gathering of resources.
                      </li>
                      <li>
                       Population growth.
                      </li>
                     </ol>
                    </li>
                    <li>
                     This server does not end;  has no rounds;  is a permanent server
                     <dl>
                      <dd>
                       Good for ten (10) years until the year 2028, according to some of the foreign language forums.
                       <br/>
                      </dd>
                     </dl>
                    </li>
                   </ol>
                  </li>
                 </ol>
                 <h2>
                  <span class="mw-headline" id="May_22.2C_2018">
                   May 22, 2018
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <table class="plainlinks quotation2">
                  <caption>
                  </caption>
                  <tr>
                   <td style="vertical-align: top; color: #B2B7F2; font-size: 50px; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight: bold; text-align: left; padding: 2px 2px; padding-top: 4px;">
                    “
                   </td>
                   <td>
                    <i>
                     <b>
                      War Server incoming...with a special twist though...
                     </b>
                    </i>
                    <p>
                     Hello Players
                    </p>
                    <p>
                     <br/>
                     Tomorrow we will start a new War server.
                    </p>
                    <p>
                     <br/>
                     The settings are as known:
                    </p>
                    <dl>
                     <dd>
                      increased population growth
                     </dd>
                     <dd>
                      reduced training and travel times for spies
                     </dd>
                     <dd>
                      reduced cooldowns and durations of miracles
                     </dd>
                     <dd>
                      increased fallback times
                     </dd>
                     <dd>
                      faster loading times, including with pillaging
                     </dd>
                     <dd>
                      increased building times
                     </dd>
                     <dd>
                      gold pillaging
                     </dd>
                     <dd>
                      increased gathering of resources
                     </dd>
                    </dl>
                    <p>
                     The new part: the server doesn't end.
                    </p>
                    <p>
                     Enjoy
                     <i>
                     </i>
                    </p>
                   </td>
                   <td style="vertical-align: bottom; color: #B2B7F2; font-size: 50px; font-family: 'Times New Roman',serif; font-weight: bold; text-align: right; padding: 2px 2px; padding-top: 4px;">
                    ”
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                  <tr>
                   <td>
                   </td>
                   <td>
                    <span style="margin-left: 3em;">
                     --
                     <a class="external text" href="https://board.en.ikariam.gameforge.com/index.php/User/45988-Hera/" rel="nofollow">
                      -Hera-
                     </a>
                     EN Board Administrator (
                     <small>
                      <a class="external text" href="https://board.en.ikariam.gameforge.com/index.php/Thread/29703-War-Server-incoming-with-a-special-twist-though/" rel="nofollow">
                       <i>
                        source
                       </i>
                      </a>
                     </small>
                     )
                    </span>
                   </td>
                   <td>
                   </td>
                  </tr>
                 </table>
                 <dl>
                  <dt>
                   Note:
                  </dt>
                  <dd>
                   This server will be added to
                   <b>
                    ALL
                   </b>
                   communities, not just the one server for each language group!
                   <br/>
                  </dd>
                 </dl>
                </td>
               </tr>
              </table>

             <table class="multicol" style="background: transparent; width: 100%; margin: auto;">
              <tr>
               <td style="text-align: left; vertical-align: top; width: 50%; padding-left:0px;">
                <h2 style="padding: 0.2em 0.4em; margin: 0 0 10px 0; border: 1px solid #EEC; background: #DC8; color: #FEA; font-weight: bold; font-size: 120%;">
                 <span class="mw-headline" id="Featured_article">
                  Featured article
                 </span>
                </h2>
                The
                <b>
                 <a href="/wiki/Beginner%27s_Guide" title="Beginner's Guide">
                  Beginner's Guide
                 </a>
                </b>
                is one of the best starting points available today for anyone wanting to jump right into
                <a href="/wiki/Ikariam" title="Ikariam">
                 Ikariam
                </a>
                .
                <p>
                 Covering the major game concepts, such as
                 <a href="/wiki/Resources" title="Resources">
                  resources
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Building" title="Building">
                  buildings
                 </a>
                 , and
                 <a href="/wiki/Research" title="Research">
                  research
                 </a>
                 , the
                 <a href="/wiki/Category:Guides" title="Category:Guides">
                  guide
                 </a>
                 then goes on to walk a new player through all the first few steps to get them started off right.
                 <br/>
                </p>
                <p>
                 <br style="clear: left;"/>
                </p>
                <p>
                 <br/>
                </p>
                <p>
                 <br/>
                </p>
               </td>
               <td style="text-align: left; vertical-align: top; width: 50%; padding-left:0px;">

                    <h2>
                     <span class="mw-headline" id="Bugfixes">
                      Bugfixes
                     </span>
                    </h2>
                    <ol>
                     <li>
                      It is no longer possible for the remaining duration of a
                      <a href="/wiki/Units" title="Units">
                       troop
                      </a>
                      movement to be displayed incorrectly as a result of timezone differences
                     </li>
                     <li>
                      A bug where
                      <a href="/wiki/Unit-ship:Balloon-Bombardier" title="Unit-ship:Balloon-Bombardier">
                       Balloon Bombardiers
                      </a>
                      were displayed with false expansion levels in battle reports has been resolved
                     </li>
                    </ol>

            <div class="tabbertab" title="Helping out">
             <p>
             </p>
             <p style="text-align: right; font-size: 130%;">
              <i>
               <b>
                <a href="/wiki/Special:AllPages" title="Special:AllPages">
                 See all pages
                </a>
               </b>
              </i>
             </p>
             <div class="plainlinks">
              <h2 style="padding: 0.2em 0.4em; margin: 0 0 10px 0; border: 1px solid #EEC; background: #FEA; color: #DC8; font-weight: bold; font-size: 120%;">
               <span class="mw-headline" id="We_need_you_and_your_help.21">
                We need you and your help!
               </span>
              </h2>
              <p>
               As you probably know, some of the
               <a href="/wiki/Ikariam" title="Ikariam">
                Ikariam
               </a>
               game
               <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Server" title="Server">
                servers
               </a>
               were recently updated to 7.9.2. This patch brought a few changes. Do you want to help make this wiki better by doing your part? You don't have to know everything about editing, you don't even have to be registered. All you need is to have some information we don't have. So, maybe you can help by filling the pages that are
               <a href="/wiki/Category:Missing_information" title="Category:Missing information">
                missing information
               </a>
               ,
               <a href="/wiki/Category:Article_stubs" title="Category:Article stubs">
                stubs
               </a>
               or
               <a href="/wiki/Category:Needs_updating" title="Category:Needs updating">
                needing updates
               </a>
               . Please look at some pages which are missing information or need updating:
              </p>
              <table class="multicol" style="background: transparent; width: 100%; margin: auto;">
               <tr>
                <td style="text-align: left; vertical-align: top; width: 33.33%; padding-left:0px;">
                 <dl>
                  <dt>
                   Pages
                   <a href="/wiki/Category:Missing_information" title="Category:Missing information">
                    missing information
                   </a>

                  </dt>
                 </dl>

                   </a>
                  </li>

                    Ikariam:List of Administrators/Game
                   </a>

              <p>
               <i>

                <a class="text" href="http://ikariam.wikia.com/wiki/Main_Page?action=purge">
                 refresh them!
                </a>

              <h2 style="padding: 0.2em 0.4em; margin: 0 0 10px 0; border: 1px solid #EEC; background: #DC8; color: #FEA; font-weight: bold; font-size: 120%;">
               <span class="mw-headline" id="Helping_out">
                Helping out
               </span>
              </h2>
              <p>
               To write a new article (after doing a search to check whether an existing article has a similar name), just enter the title in the box below.
              </p>
              <div class="createbox" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align:center">
               <p>
               </p>
               <form action="/index.php" class="createboxForm" method="get" name="createbox">
                <input name="action" type="hidden" value="create"/>
                <input name="prefix" type="hidden" value=""/>
                <input name="preload" type="hidden" value=""/>
                <input name="editintro" type="hidden" value=""/>
                <input class="createboxInput" name="title" size="24" type="text" value=""/>
                <input class="createboxButton" name="create" type="submit" value="Create a new article"/>
               </form>
              </div>
              <dl>
               <dt>
                Not sure where to start?
               </dt>
               <dd>
               </dd>
              </dl>
              <ul>
               <li>
                Find out more about the wiki on the
                <b>
                 <a href="/wiki/Ikariam:About" title="Ikariam:About">
                  About
                 </a>
                </b>
                page.
               </li>
               <li>
                If you are new to wikis, check out the
                <b>
                 <a class="extiw" href="//community.wikia.com/wiki/Help:Tutorial_1" title="wikia:Help:Tutorial 1">
                  tutorial
                 </a>
                </b>
                .
               </li>
              </ul>
              <dl>
               <dt>
                Adding content
               </dt>
               <dd>
               </dd>
              </dl>
              <ul>
               <li>
                Some great places to start helping with the WikIkariam are to update
                <b>
                 <a href="/wiki/Category:Article_stubs" title="Category:Article stubs">
                  "Stubs"
                 </a>
                </b>
                and pages marked
                <b>
                 <a href="/wiki/Category:Missing_information" title="Category:Missing information">
                  "Missing Information"
                 </a>
                </b>
                . You can also help out by writing
                <b>
                 <a href="/wiki/Special:WantedPages" title="Special:WantedPages">
                  "Wanted Articles"
                 </a>
                </b>
                . Don't be shy, get in there, and we can fix anything that goes wrong.
               </li>
               <li>
                Uploading
                <a href="/wiki/Category:Images" title="Category:Images">
                 images
                </a>
                is another really easy way to help out - see the
                <b>
                 <a href="/wiki/Special:Upload" title="Special:Upload">
                  Upload
                 </a>
                </b>
                page!
               </li>
               <li>
                You can find a list of time-saving
                <b>
                 templates
                </b>
                in
                <a href="/wiki/Category:Templates" title="Category:Templates">
                 Category:Templates
                </a>
                !
               </li>
              </ul>
              <dl>
               <dt>
                Talk and more...
               </dt>
               <dd>
               </dd>
              </dl>
              <ul>
               <li>
                If you need to ask for help or can answer someone's plea, check out the
                <b>
                 <a href="/wiki/Forum:Help_desk" title="Forum:Help desk">
                  Help desk
                 </a>
                </b>
                .
               </li>
               <li>
                To see what the community is working on, to give feedback, or just to say Hi, check out the
                <b>
                 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Forum:Watercooler" title="Forum:Watercooler">
                  Watercooler
                 </a>
                </b>
                .
               </li>
               <li>
                <a href="/wiki/Special:Insights" title="Special:Insights">
                 Statistics
                </a>
                show the growth of the wiki and who is doing the work (and who has stopped!)
               </li>
              </ul>
              <p>
               <br/>
               <br/>
              </p>
             </div>

              <ul>
               <li>
                You should link to these wikis by using the {{
                <a href="/wiki/Template:Alt-Lang" title="Template:Alt-Lang">
                 <b>
                  Alt-Lang
                 </b>
                </a>
                |
                <span style="color: gray;">
                 <i>
                  <b>
                   language-tag
                  </b>
                 </i>
                </span>
                |
                <span style="color: gray;">
                 <i>
                  <b>
                   pagename
                  </b>
                 </i>
                </span>
                }} template (if
                <b>
                 pagename
                </b>
                is blank it will link to the
                <i>
                 Main Page
                </i>
                of the wiki) - the template will automatically add the interwiki language-tags to the page.
               </li>
               <li>
                Another way to link to them by using the language tag format (at the bottom of most all pages)
                <code>
                 [[language-tag:PAGENAME]]
                </code>
                or as and example:
                <code>
                 [[es:]]
                </code>
                will link to the
                <i>
                 Main Page
                </i>
                of the
                <a class="extiw" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" title="wikipedia:Spanish language">
                 Spanish language
                </a>
                wiki and
                <code>
                 [[es:pagename]]
                </code>
                will link to
                <b>
                 pagename
                </b>
                on the wiki.
                <ul>
                 <li>
                  Please try to
                  <b>
                   AVOID
                  </b>
                  using this method, and try to use {{
                  <a href="/wiki/Template:Alt-Lang" title="Template:Alt-Lang">
                   <b>
                    Alt-Lang
                   </b>
                  </a>
                  }} instead.
                 </li>
                </ul>
               </li>
               <li>
                <b>
                 Note
                </b>
                : Do
                <b>
                 NOT
                </b>
                use
                <a href="/wiki/Help:Interwiki_links" title="Help:Interwiki links">
                 interwiki linking
                </a>
                codes and {{
                <a href="/wiki/Template:Alt-Lang" title="Template:Alt-Lang">
                 <b>
                  Alt-Lang
                 </b>
                </a>
                }} on the same page - this will cause the language box to have
                <b>
                 duplicate
                </b>
                language entries (both will work if you used the right coding for your entries). If a page has
                <a href="/wiki/Help:Interwiki_links" title="Help:Interwiki links">
                 interwiki links
                </a>
                already on it, please add the {{
                <a href="/wiki/Template:Alt-Lang" title="Template:Alt-Lang">
                 <b>
                  Alt-Lang
                 </b>
                </a>
                }} template using the language tags from the interwiki links and then
                <b>
                 REMOVE
                </b>
                the interwiki links.
               </li>
              </ul>
